emacs-common in Fedora 32

This page displays detailed information for a specific version of emacs-common. You might want go back to the main page of emacs-common.

Changelog

Date Author Change
2020-08-18 Jan Synáček - 1:27.1-2 - use make macros (original patch provided by Tom Stellard) - https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Changes/UseMakeBuildInstallMacro
2020-08-11 Bhavin Gandhi - 1:27.1-1 - emacs-27.1 is available (#1867841) - Add systemd-devel to support Type=notify in unit file - Build with Cairo and Jansson support - Remove ImageMagick dependency as it's no longer used
2020-04-16 Dan Čermák - 1:26.3-3 - Drop dependency on GConf2
2020-01-28 Fedora Release Engineering - 1:26.3-2 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_32_Mass_Rebuild
2019-09-08 Maximiliano Sandoval - 1:26.3-1 - emacs-26.3 is available (#1747101)
2019-07-24 Fedora Release Engineering - 1:26.2-2 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_31_Mass_Rebuild
2019-04-17 Jan Synáček - 1:26.2-1 - emacs-26.2 is available (#1699434)
2019-01-31 Fedora Release Engineering - 1:26.1-8 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_30_Mass_Rebuild
2018-08-28 Michael Cronenworth - 1:26.1-7 - Rebuild for new ImageMagick 6.9.10
